 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="tx661113_1"></A>PART I </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>INTRODUCTION </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unless
otherwise indicated, all references herein to &#147;Ericsson,&#148; the &#147;Company,&#148; &#147;the Group,&#148; &#147;we,&#148; &#147;us,&#148; or &#147;our&#148; or &#147;our company&#148; are references to Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson and
its consolidated subsidiaries. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This document is our Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> for the year ended
December&nbsp;31, 2018 (the &#147;2018 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F&#148;).</FONT> Reference is made to the English version of our Swedish Annual Report for 2018, with certain adjustments made to comply with U.S. requirements, which is
attached hereto as Exhibit 15.1 (the &#147;2018 Swedish Annual Report&#148;). Only (i)&nbsp;the information included in this 2018 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F,</FONT> (ii)&nbsp;the information in the 2018 Swedish Annual Report that is
incorporated by reference in this 2018 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F,</FONT> and (iii)&nbsp;the exhibits to the 2018 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> that are required to be filed pursuant to the Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> shall be deemed to be filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission for any purpose, including incorporation by reference into the Registration Statement on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">F-3</FONT>
filed on March&nbsp;27, 2018 (File <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">No.&nbsp;333-223954)</FONT> and any other document filed by us pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, which incorporates by reference the 2018 Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F.</FONT> Any information in the 2018 Swedish Annual Report that is not referenced in the 2018 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> or filed as an exhibit thereto shall not be deemed to be so incorporated
by reference. Certain industry, technical and financial terms used in this 2018 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> are defined in the subsections entitled &#147;Glossary&#148; and &#147;Financial Terminology&#148; of the 2018 Swedish
Annual Report, which are incorporated herein by reference. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Market data and certain industry forecasts used herein were obtained from
internal surveys, market research, publicly available information and industry publications. While we believe that market research, publicly available information and industry publications we use are reliable, we have not independently verified
market and industry data from third-party sources. Moreover, while we believe our internal surveys are reliable, they have not been verified by any independent source. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information included on <U>www.ericsson.com</U> and other websites that appear in this 2018 Form
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> is not incorporated by reference herein. From time to time, we may use our website as a channel of distribution of material company information. Financial and other material information regarding our
company is routinely posted on and accessible at <U>www.ericsson.com</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P>

including statements reflecting management&#146;s current views relating to the growth of the market, future market conditions, future events, financial condition, and expected operational and financial performance, including, in particular the
following: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>General facts on the company </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Legal and
commercial name of the Parent Company:</B> Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson (publ). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Organization number:</B> 556016-0680 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Legal form of the Parent Company:</B> A Swedish limited liability company, organized under the Swedish Companies Act. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Country of incorporation:</B> Sweden. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Date of
incorporation:</B> The Parent Company was incorporated on August&nbsp;18, 1918, as a result of a merger between AB LM Ericsson&nbsp;&amp; Co. and Stockholms Allm&auml;nna Telefon AB. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Domicile:</B> Our registered office is Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson, SE&#150;164 83 Stockholm, Sweden. Our headquarters are located at Torshamnsgatan
21, Kista, Sweden. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Telephone number:</B> +46 10 719 0000 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Website:</B> <U>www.ericsson.com</U>. The information included on our website is not incorporated herein by reference. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Agent in the US:</B> Ericsson Inc., Vice President Legal Affairs, 6300 Legacy Drive, Plano, Texas 75024. Telephone number: +1 972 583 0000. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Shares:</B> Ericsson&#146;s Class&nbsp;A and Class&nbsp;B shares are traded on Nasdaq Stockholm. In the US, our American Depository Shares (ADS), each
representing one underlying Class&nbsp;B share, are traded on NASDAQ New York. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Parent company operations:</B> The business of the parent company,
Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson, consists mainly of corporate management, holding company functions and internal banking activities. Our parent company operations also include customer credit management activities performed by Ericsson Credit AB on
a commission basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Subsidiaries and associated companies:</B> For a list of our significant subsidiaries, please see &#147;Item 4C.
Investments&#148;. In addition to our joint venture <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ST-Ericsson</FONT> (up until August&nbsp;2, 2013), we are engaged in a number of minor joint ventures and cooperative arrangements. For more information regarding
risks associated with joint ventures, strategic alliances and third-party agreements, please see &#147;Item 3D. Financials&#150;Risk Factors&#151;Market, Technology and Business Risks&#148;. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Company history and development </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Innovating to
empower people, business and society </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our origins date back to 1876 when Alexander Graham Bell filed a patent application in the United
States for the telephone. The same year, Lars Magnus Ericsson opened a small workshop in Stockholm to repair telegraph instruments and sell his own telephone equipment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Today, Ericsson enables communications service providers to capture the full value of connectivity. The company&#146;s portfolio spans
Networks, Digital Services, Managed Services, and Emerging Business and is designed to help our customers go digital, increase efficiency and find new revenue streams. Ericsson&#146;s investments in innovation have delivered the benefits of
telephony and mobile broadband to billions of people around the world. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The SEC maintains an Internet site that contains reports, proxy and information
statements, and other information regarding issuers that file electronically with the SEC: http://www.sec.gov. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Disclosure pursuant to Section&nbsp;219 of the Iran Threat Reduction and Syria Human Rights Act of
2012 (ITRA) </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson has conducted business in Iran/Persia since the late nineteenth century, opened an office in Iran in 1973 and later
established a local subsidiary in the country. Ericsson strongly believes in enabling communication for all and believes that access to communications can enable the right to health, education and freedom of expression. Ericsson&#146;s business
activities in Iran principally involve the sale of communications infrastructure related products and services, including support, installation and maintenance services. Ericsson&#146;s exports from the European Union (the &#147;EU&#148;) to Iran
are performed under export licenses from the Swedish Agency for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Proliferation</FONT> and Export Controls and in compliance with applicable economic sanctions and export controls. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Due to its operations in Iran, and having staff permanently in the country, Ericsson has contacts with its local customers and retains certain local
suppliers, including banks, and service providers. In addition, Ericsson has other dealings incidental to its local activities, such as making payments for taxes, salaries, rents, utilities and office and similar supplies as well for local
accommodation and transportation and customs related services. As a result, Ericsson has contact with companies and public functions that may be owned or controlled by the government of Iran. While Ericsson seeks to obtain information regarding the
actual business names and ownership of customers and other counterparties in Iran through its policies and procedures designed to ensure that Ericsson &#147;knows its customers&#148;, it is challenging to determine ownership and control with
certainty, particularly with respect to determining whether an entity engaged in commercial activities is owned or controlled by the government. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During
2018, Ericsson sold communications infrastructure related products and services in Iran to the following telecommunications companies operating in the country: Farabord Dadehavare Iranian (&#147;Farabord&#148;) (relating to purchase orders received
before May 2018), Mobile Communication Company of Iran (&#147;MCCI&#148;), and MTN Irancell. During 2018, Ericsson&#146;s gross revenue (reported as net sales) related to sales to Farabord, MCCI and MTNIrancell in Iran was approximately
SEK&nbsp;990&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson does not normally allocate net profit (reported as net income) on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">country-by-country</FONT></FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">activity-by-activity</FONT></FONT> basis, other than as set forth in Ericsson&#146;s consolidated financial statements
prepared in accordance with IFRS as issued by the IASB. However, Ericsson has estimated that its operating income (income before taxes and financial net) from such sales was negative, after internal cost allocation approximately SEK <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">-820&nbsp;million</FONT> during 2018. Ericsson always strives to honor its engagements with existing customers in compliance with applicable export controls, sanctions and other laws, rules and regulations, but it is clear
that the U.S. withdrawal from the Joint Comprehensive Plan of Action (the &#147;JCPOA&#148;) has impacted the overall possibility of doing business in Iran. Ericsson has carefully evaluated the implications of the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-introduced</FONT> sanctions (caused by the withdrawal by the US from the JCPOA) and continues to monitor developments in this area as it relates to the ability to continue delivering products and services to
customers. Since the US withdrawal from the JCPOA, Ericsson is winding down its business and organization significantly but still continues to provide the two main mobile carriers, MCCI and MTN Irancell with support critical for the network to
function and to fulfill engagements with these carriers entered into before May&nbsp;8, 2018. As Ericsson fulfil contractual obligations with regard to contracts entered into before the US withdrawal from the JCPOA, Ericsson may, during a wind down
period need to interact with other counterparties. Ericsson continues to explore, including with EU and US authorities, whether and how the disruptive impact on the ability to maintain and support the operations of existing networks of MCCI and MTN
Irancell can be minimized and by doing so, endeavor to avoid undue impacts on the access of the people of Iran to humanitarian items/basic services such as telecommunications. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In some instances, Ericsson has had to arrange performance bonds or similar financial guarantees to secure Ericsson&#146;s performance of obligations under
the commercial agreements Ericsson has entered into relating to the business in Iran. In such instances, Ericsson usually engages its banks outside Iran, who in turn engage local banks in the country. These local banks include Tejarat Bank, Melli
Bank, Parsian Bank and Saderat Bank. Although some bonds and guarantees are still in place, no new performance bonds or similar guarantees involving these four banks with respect to Ericsson&#146;s business activities in Iran were issued during
2018. During the first quarter of 2018, payment was made by Ericsson, via one of Ericsson&#146;s banks outside Iran, to Bank Mellat, under a previously issued performance bond. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During 2018, existing bank guarantees issued by Bank Mellat, Maskan Bank, Parsian Bank, Post Bank of Iran
and Tejarat Bank (local banks in Iran) to cover Ericsson&#146;s obligations under customer contracts or tender rules were extended in time. Further, some payments made to Ericsson&#146;s local subsidiary and payments required to be made by the local
subsidiary to suppliers involve banks that may be controlled by the government of Iran. Ericsson also received payments from customers in Iran to Ericsson&#146;s accounts outside Iran. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="tx661113_12"></A><A NAME="exind661113_1a"></A>C. Organizational Structure </B></P>

list of shareholdings, prepared in accordance with the Swedish Annual Accounts Act and filed with the Swedish Companies Registration Office (Bolagsverket), may be obtained upon request to: Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson, External Reporting, <FONT

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Primary manufacturing and assembly facilities </I></B></P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="27%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Regulatory, Compliance and Corporate Governance risks </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><U>Operating results for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2016 and 2017 </U></I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Full-year highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reported sales decreased by &#150;7%
to SEK 205.4 (220.3) billion with a decline in all segments. IPR licensing revenues amounted to&nbsp;SEK 8.3 (10.3) billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income declined to
SEK &#150;34.7 (5.2) billion, mainly due to write-down of assets as&nbsp;well as provisions and customer project adjustments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash flow from operating
activities was SEK 9.6 (14.0) billion. Free cash flow amounted to&nbsp;SEK 5.1 (0.3) billion. Net cash at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> was SEK 34.7 (31.2) billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board of Directors approved a dividend for 2017 of SEK 1.00 (1.00) per share at the AGM. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business in 2017 </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In 2017, net sales decreased by
&#150;7% with a&nbsp;decline in all segments as described in more detail below. The sales decrease in Networks was mainly due to lower demand for radio access network equipment. The sales decrease in Digital services and Other was mainly due to
lower sales of legacy products. The sales decline in Manages Services was mainly due to a renewed contract in North America in 2016 that was reduced in scope. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">IPR licensing revenues were SEK 8.3 (10.3)&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In
2017 a focused business strategy was set and a new organizational structure was implemented. In addition, the company initiated a cost saving program with the target to reduce annual cost by SEK 10&nbsp;billion by mid 2018. Together, this resulted
in significant restructuring charges of SEK &#150;8.5 (&#150;7.6) billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Due to technology and portfolio shifts, the company has reduced the
capitalization of development expenses for product platforms and software releases and the deferral of hardware costs. As a consequence, higher amortization than capitalization of development expenses and higher recognition than deferral of hardware
costs had a negative impact on operating income of SEK &#150;2.9 (3.8)&nbsp;billion. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income was SEK &#150;34.7 - (5.2)&nbsp;billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson delivered a full-year cash flow from operating activities of SEK 9.6 (14.0) billion. Free cash flow amounted to SEK 5.1 (0.3) billion. Net cash at
year end was SEK&nbsp;34.7 (31.2) billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial highlights </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Net sales </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reported sales decreased by SEK
&#150;14.9&nbsp;billion or &#150;7%, with a SEK &#150;7.8&nbsp;billion or &#150;6% decrease in Networks, SEK &#150;4.0&nbsp;billion or &#150;9% decrease in Digital Services, SEK &#150;2.3&nbsp;billion or &#150;8% in Managed Services and SEK
&#150;0.8&nbsp;billion or &#150;9% in segment Emerging Business and Other. The sales decrease in Networks was mainly due to lower demand for radio access network (RAN) equipment, which was estimated by an external source to decline by &#150;8% for
full-year 2017. The sales decrease in segments Digital Services and Emerging Business and Other was mainly due to lower sales of legacy products. The sales decline in Managed Services was mainly due to a renewed contract in North America in 2016
that was reduced in scope. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">IPR licensing revenues amounted to SEK 8.3 (10.3) billion. The revenues in 2016 were positively impacted by two signed
contracts which included certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> items. The baseline for the current IPR licensing contract portfolio is approximately SEK 7&nbsp;billion on an annual basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The sales mix by commodity was: software 21% (22%), hardware 35% (33%) and services 44% (45%). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Gross margin </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross margin declined to 23.3% (29.6%) due
to provisions and customer projects adjustments, write-down of assets and lower IPR licensing revenues at SEK 8.3 (10.3) billion. In&nbsp;addition, restructuring charges included in&nbsp;the gross margin increased to SEK &#150;5.2
(&#150;3.5)&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Due to technology and portfolio shifts, the company has reduced the capitalization of development expenses for software
releases and the deferral of hardware costs. As a consequence, higher amortization than capitalization of development expenses and higher recognition than deferral of hardware costs had a negative impact on gross income of SEK&nbsp;&#150;2.6
(&#150;0.5) billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Operating expenses </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating
expenses increased to SEK &#150;70.6 (&#150;60.5) billion, mainly as a result of provisions and customer project adjustments and write-down of assets. In addition, operating expenses increased due to higher amortized than capitalized development
expenses with a negative effect on operating expenses of SEK &#150;0.3 (4.3) billion. Operating expenses included restructuring charges of SEK &#150;3.3 (&#150;4.1) billion of which the sale of the global ICT center in Montreal generated a
restructuring charge of SEK &#150;1.3&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Other operating income and expenses </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Other operating income was SEK 1.2 (2.0) billion. In 2017, the power modules business was divested, which resulted in a gain of SEK 0.3&nbsp;billion. Other
operating expenses declined to SEK &#150;13.3 (&#150;1.6) billion negatively impacted by write-down of goodwill.As of 2017, the funding of foreign exchange forecast hedging is managed through foreign exchange loans (USD) instead of foreign exchange
derivates. Therefore, revaluation and realization effects are included in financial expenses instead of other operating income and expenses. In 2016, the currency hedge contract effects impacted other operating income and expenses by
SEK&nbsp;&#150;0.9&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Restructuring charges and cost savings </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges amounted to SEK &#150;8.5 (&#150;7.6) billion. This was lower than the earlier estimate of SEK 9&#150;10&nbsp;billion. The restructuring
charges mainly relate to cost savings. The target is to implement such savings with an annual run rate effect of at least SEK 10&nbsp;billion by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-2018.</FONT> Approximately 30% of the cost savings are targeted
at&nbsp;administrative expenses and 70% at cost of&nbsp;sales. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total restructuring charges for 2018 are estimated to be SEK 5&#150;7&nbsp;billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Consequences of technology and portfolio shifts </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Due to
technology and portfolio shifts the company is reducing the capitalization of development expenses for product platforms and software releases and the deferral of hardware costs. As a consequence, higher amortization than capitalization of
development expenses and higher recognition than deferral of hardware costs had a negative impact on operating income. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>

</DIV></Center>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Operating income (loss) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income (loss) decreased to SEK &#150;34.7 (5.2) billion, mainly due to write-down of assets of SEK, provisions and customer project adjustments and
lower sales. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition, higher amortization than capitalization of development expenses and higher recognition than deferral of hardware costs had a
negative impact on operating income of SEK &#150;2.9 (3.8) billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating margin was &#150;16.9% (2.4%). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial net </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The financial net improved to SEK
&#150;1.2 (&#150;2.3) billion, mainly due to lower negative effects of foreign exchange revaluation. Lower interest rates partly offset the improvement. New borrowings have been signed on more favorable terms and risk reduction, in both currency
exchange and interest rates, has been improved in 2017. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The currency hedge effects, which derive from the hedge loan balance in USD, impacted financial
net by SEK 0.5&nbsp;billion. The SEK has strengthened against the USD between December&nbsp;31, 2016 (SEK/USD rate 9.06) and December&nbsp;31, 2017 (SEK/USD rate 8.20). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Taxes </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Taxes were SEK 3.5 (&#150;1.9) billion following
the negative net income. The effective tax rate was 10%, negatively impacted by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-deductible</FONT> expenses (mainly goodwill impairment), by revaluation of deferred tax assets due to the change in U.S. corporate
income tax rate, and by an allowance related to certain Swedish tax assets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Net income (loss) and EPS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net income (loss) decreased to SEK &#150;32.4 (1.0) billion, for the same reasons as for the decrease in operating income. EPS diluted was SEK &#150;9.94
(0.25) and EPS <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(non-IFRS)</FONT> was SEK &#150;3.24 (2.39). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Employees </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The number of employees on December&nbsp;31, 2017 was 100,735, a net reduction of more than 10,000 employees in 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business results &#150; Segments </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Networks </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Networks represented 64% (64%) of net sales in 2017. The segment delivers products and services that are needed for mobile and fixed communication, several
generations of radio networks and transmission networks. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net sales </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales as reported decreased by &#150;6% YoY to SEK 132.3 (140.1) billion.. The decrease was mainly due to lower operator investments in mobile broadband, both
products and services. In addition, the IPR licensing business declined to SEK 6.8 (8.4) billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross margin </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross income decreased to SEK 43.4 (46.2) billion and gross margin decreased to 32.8% (33.2%). The gross margin decrease was mainly due to provisions and
customer project adjustments made in the year. Higher amortization than capitalization of development expenses and higher recognition than deferral of hardware costs, together amounting to SEK &#150;1.5 (0.2) billion, also had a negative impact on
gross margin. This is a consequence of technology and portfolio shifts. Gross margin was positively impacted by higher hardware margins. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income decreased to SEK 10.5 (16.7) billion due to lower sales with lower IPR licensing revenues, provisions and customer project adjustments,
write-down of assets made in the year as well as increased operating expenses. The higher operating expenses are partly due to the strategic decision to increase investments in Networks&#146; R&amp;D. Higher amortization than capitalization of
development expenses and higher recognition than deferral of hardware costs together amounted to SEK &#150;1.5 (1.0) billion. Restructuring charges were SEK &#150;4.8 (&#150;3.4) billion. Operating margin decreased to 7.9% (11.9%). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Digital Services </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Digital Services represented 19% (19%)
of net sales in 2017. The segment is providing solutions for operators&#146; digital transformation journeys across the support systems BSS and OSS, Telecom Core, and IT Cloud domains through a combination of products, technology and expertise in
networks, software, cloud, and business processes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net sales </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales as reported decreased by &#150;9% to SEK 38.8 (42.8) billion, due to lower sales of legacy products and related services, primarily in OSS, BSS and
Packet Core. IPR and licensing revenues declined to SEK 1.5 (1.8) billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross margin </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross income declined to SEK 4.7 (15.6) billion and gross margin decreased to 12.1% (35.0%). The gross margin decrease was mainly due to write-down of assets
as well as provisions and customer project adjustments. In addition, there was a negative impact from higher costs in ongoing large transformation projects and from reduced sales of legacy products including related services. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income (loss) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income (loss) declined to
&#150;27.3 (&#150;7.1) billion, mainly due to write-down of assets as well as provisions and customer project adjustments. In addition, operating income was negatively impacted by lower gross margin and lower sales. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The full-year negative impact of higher amortized than capitalized development expenses was SEK &#150;1.3 (2.1) billion. This was partly offset by cost
reductions, impacting both R&amp;D and selling and administrative expenses. Restructuring charges were SEK &#150;2.5 (&#150;3.2) billion. Operating margin declined to &#150;70.4% (&#150;15.3%). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Managed Services </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Managed Services represented 13% (13%)
of&nbsp;net sales in 2017. The segment delivers managed services and network optimization to telecom operators. Through these offerings, customers entrust Ericsson to run the operations of their network/IT systems and optimize network performance.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net sales </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales as reported decreased by &#150;8% to SEK
26.5 (28.8) billion, mainly a result of the earlier communicated rescoped Managed Services Networks contract in North America. In addition, sales were negatively impacted by completion of 23 contracts, out of the 42 identified to be exited,
renegotiated or transformed. Sales in Managed Services IT showed good growth. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross margin </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross income declined to SEK &#150;1.6 (1.2) billion. Gross margin was &#150;5.9% (4.0%), negatively affected by provisions and customer project adjustments as
well as an asset write-down made in the year. In addition, gross margin was negatively impacted by lower sales and negative development in contracts identified to be exited, renegotiated or transformed. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income (loss) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income (loss) decreased to
SEK&nbsp;&#150;4.1 (&#150;0.3) billion due to lower sales, reduced gross margin and increased operating&nbsp;expenses. Restructuring charges amounted to SEK &#150;0.7 (&#150;0.4 ) billion. Operating margin was &#150;15.4% (&#150;1.7%). </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">15 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Emerging Business and Other </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Segment Emerging Business and Other represented 4% (4%) of net sales in 2017. The segment consists of four businesses; Media solutions, Red Bee Media, Emerging
business and iconectiv. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net sales </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales as reported
decreased by &#150;9% to SEK 7.9 (8.7) billion, due to lower sales in Media Solutions, where sales of legacy products and related services declined. Red Bee Media sales declined by &#150;8% YoY, due to renegotiations and scope changes of contracts.
The decline was partly offset by growth in Emerging-Business and iconectiv. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross margin </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross income declined to SEK 1.4 (2.2) billion and gross margin decreased to 17.5% (25.5%). The gross margin decrease was mainly due to write-down of assets.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income (loss) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income (loss) declined
to &#150;13.8 (&#150;4.0) billion, mainly due to write-down of intangible assets and goodwill. Operating income (loss) excluding asset write-downs declined, mainly due to increased investments in Emerging Business, higher amortized than capitalized
development expenses of SEK &#150;0.1 (0.7) billion and lower sales. The decline was partly offset by cost reductions in both Media Solutions and Red Bee Media. Restructuring charges amounted to SEK &#150;0.5 (&#150;0.6 ) billion. Operating margin
was &#150;175.7% (&#150;46.2%). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business results &#150; Market areas </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>South East Asia, Oceania and India </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales declined due to
lower mobile broadband investments in Thailand, Indonesia and India. Growth in Digital Services was driven by growth in Australia, Singapore and Indonesia, mainly related to core network solutions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>North East Asia </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in Mainland China declined due to
reduced LTE investments. Sales in Taiwan declined following a new network deployment for one operator in 2016. The markets in Korea and Japan stabilized and Ericsson increased its market share in Japan. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>North America </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">North America sales increased with
increased networks sales, driven by expasions to cater for increased data traffic. The increase was partly offset by lower managed services sales due to a renegotiated large managed services contract with reduced scope. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Europe and Latin America </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales declined, mainly due to
timing of major projects in Mexico and termination of a large contract in Italy. In addition, capex constraints in mobile broadband in Europe impacted sales negatively, as operators focus investments in fixed infrastructure. The decline was
partially offset by network modernizations in Brazil. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Middle East and Africa </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales declined in a challenging macroeconomic environment with cautious investments in broadband. Digital Services sales declined slightly. Managed Services
sales declined due to effects of completed contract reviews. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Other</B><B><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1)</SUP></B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales declined due to lower IPR licensing revenues and lower sales in Media Solutions, where sales of legacy products and related services declined. IPR
licensing revenues amounted to SEK 8.3 (10.3) billion. IPR licensing revenues in 2016 were positively impacted by two signed contracts which included certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> items. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">16 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">See &#147;Item 8.B. Financial Information &#150; Significant Changes&#148; herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><U>Balance sheet and other performance indicators for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2016 and 2017 </U></I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Cash flow </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash flow from operating activities was SEK 9.6
(14.0) billion. The decline was due to lower income and increased cash outlays related to restructuring charges. The cash flow was supported by a reduction of operating assets. Cash outlays related to restructuring charges were SEK &#150;5.3
(&#150;2.4) billion. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">17 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash flow from investing activities was impacted by investments and sale of property, plant and equipment
with a net effect of SEK &#150;2.9 (&#150;5.6) billion. In addition, product development decreased by SEK &#150;1.4 (&#150;4.5) billion due to reduced capitalization of product platform development following technology shifts. The cash flow was
supported by the sale of Power Modules and the ICT center in&nbsp;Montreal. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash flow from financing activities was positive at SEK 5.5 (&#150;11.7)
billion due to increased net borrowings of SEK 8.6&nbsp;billion. Dividends of SEK 3.4 (12.3) billion were paid out. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The increased focus on free cash flow
and release of working capital, in combination with low investing activities, resulted in a free cash flow of SEK 5.1 (0.3) billion. The more even distribution of cash flow over the year and the&nbsp;amount of free cash flow mark a clear improvement
over 2016. For the first time in&nbsp;five years, the full-year free cash flow exceeded dividend payout. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial position </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross cash increased to SEK 67.7 (57.9) billion and net cash increased to SEK 34.7 (31.2) billion. Post-employments benefits increased by SEK 1.3&nbsp;billion
due to decreased discount rates and normal service cost, offset by returns on pension assets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The average maturity of long-term borrowings as of
December&nbsp;31, 2017, was 4.4 years, compared with 3.8 years 12 months earlier. Ericsson has an unutilized Revolving Credit Facility of USD 2.0&nbsp;billion. The facility will expire in 2022. In 2017, Ericsson concluded the following financing
activities to strengthen the balance sheet and extend the average debt maturity profile: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">The company received a USD 200&nbsp;million payment relating to Francisco Partners&#146; investments for a 16.7%
ownership in Ericsson&#146;s independent subsidiary iconectiv. Due to the structure of the investment, IFRS accounting standards stipulate that the main part of the USD 200&nbsp;million should be treated as borrowings,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-current.</FONT> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Ericsson raised USD 220&nbsp;million from the Nordic Investment Bank (NIB) and USD 150&nbsp;million from the
Swedish Export Credit Corporation (SEK). The credit agreements mature in 2023 and 2025 respectively. Of these new funds, USD 98&nbsp;million replaced a&nbsp;credit with NIB that was set to mature in&nbsp;2019. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In 2017, Standard&nbsp;&amp; Poor&#146;s downgraded Ericsson&#146;s long-term rating from BBB with negative outlook to BB+ with stable outlook. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Moody&#146;s downgraded Ericsson&#146;s long-term rating from Baa3 with negative outlook to Ba2 with negative outlook. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Intangible assets </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The amount of intellectual property
rights and other intangible assets amounted to SEK 32.0 (51.1) billion, including goodwill of SEK 27.8 (43.4) billion. The goodwill impairment testing was based on the new segments that became effective as per October&nbsp;1, 2017 and resulted in a
write-down of goodwill of SEK &#150;13.0&nbsp;billion triggered by the implementation of the focused business strategy and new organizational structure. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Research and development, patents&nbsp;and&nbsp;licensing </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In 2017, R&amp;D expenses amounted to&nbsp;SEK&nbsp;37.9 (31.6) billion. The increase is mainly due to higher amortized than capitalized development expenses
with a negative effect of SEK &#150;0.3 (4.3) billion and write-down of assets. The number of R&amp;D resources were 23,600. The number of patents continued to increase and amounted to approximately 45,000 by end of 2017. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Seasonality </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company&#146;s sales, income cash flow from operations vary and between quarters, and are generally lowest in the first quarter of the year and highest in
the fourth quarter. This is mainly a&nbsp;result of the seasonal purchase-patterns of network operators </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Off-balance</FONT> sheet arrangements </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">There are currently no material <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">off-balance</FONT> sheet arrangements that have, or would be reasonably likely to have, a
current or anticipated material effect on the Company&#146;s financial condition, revenues, expenses, result of operations, liquidity, capital expenditures or capital resources. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Capital expenditures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For 2017, capital expenditure was
SEK 3.9 (6.1) billion, representing 1.9% of sales. Expenditures are largely related to test sites and equipment for R&amp;D, network operation centers and manufacturing and repair operations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson believes that the Company&#146;s property, plant and&nbsp;equipment and the facilities the Company occupies are suitable for its present needs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Annual capital expenditures are normally around 2% of sales. This corresponds to the needs for keeping and maintaining the current capacity level. The Board
of Directors reviews the Company&#146;s investment plans and proposals. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As of December&nbsp;31, 2017, no material land, buildings, machinery or equipment
were pledged as collateral for outstanding indebtedness. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Capital expenditures 2016&#150;2017 </B></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">See &#147;Item 8.B. Financial Information &#150; Significant Changes&#148;, &#147;Item 10.B.
Memorandum and Articles of Association &#150; Dividends&#148; and &#147;Item 17. Financial Statements&#148;, herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Refer also to item
8.B herein </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="tx661113_34"></A>B. Significant Changes </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Ericsson announces change to the Executive Team </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On
16&nbsp;January 2019, Ericsson announced that Helena Norrman, Senior Vice President, Chief Marketing and Communications Officer and Head of Marketing and Corporate Relations, has decided to leave Ericsson to pursue opportunities outside the company.
She will leave her position no later than June&nbsp;30, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Ericsson completes divestment of majority stake in MediaKind </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On February&nbsp;1, 2019, Ericsson announced it&nbsp;had closed the divestment of the MediaKind business to the private equity firm One Equity Partners. One
Equity Partners became majority owner, while Ericsson has 49% of the shares after the transaction on January&nbsp;31, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson anticipates that the
transaction will generate a positive impact on operating income in Q1 2019 that with current visibility is estimated to SEK 0.4 &#150; 0.6&nbsp;billion and will be reported in Segment Emerging Business and Other. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As of February&nbsp;1, 2019, Ericsson&#146;s 49% share of MediaKind results will be reported as share in earnings of JV and associated companies in segment
Emerging Business and Other. MediaKind was in 2018 reported as part of segment Emerging Business and Other, as part of Ericsson Media Solutions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Ericsson announces change to the Executive Team </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On
12&nbsp;March 2019, Ericsson announced that Rafiah Ibrahim will leave her position as Senior Vice President and Head of Market Area Middle East&nbsp;&amp; Africa and will take on a role as advisor to CEO B&ouml;rje Ekholm. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Ericsson&#146;s Annual General Meeting </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On 27&nbsp;March
2019, Ericsson held its Annual General Meeting in Stockholm, Sweden. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Decisions at the AGM 2019 included: </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="tx661113_42"></A>ITEM&nbsp;10. ADDITIONAL INFORMATION </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="tx661113_43"></A>A. Share Capital </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Not applicable. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><A NAME="tx661113_44"></A>B. Memorandum and Articles of Association </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson is registered under no. 556016&#150;0680 in the Company Register kept by the Swedish Companies Registration
Office. Our Company&#146;s objective and purposes are described in article 2 of the Articles of Association, as follows: The objects of the Company are to, directly or indirectly, develop, construct, produce, sell and deliver and in other forms
carry on trade and other commercial business related to goods, products and other equipment as well as maintenance and other services based on telecommunication and radio technology and other technologies for transference, transmission and other
communications of speech, data, images, text, other kinds of information and means of payment and to carry on other activities consistent therewith. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our Articles of Association do not stipulate anything regarding: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">a director&#146;s power to vote on a proposal, arrangement, or contract in which the director is materially
interested; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">our directors&#146; power to vote for compensation to themselves; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">retirement rules for our directors; or </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">the number of shares required for a director&#146;s qualification. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Applicable provisions are found in the Swedish Companies Act (2005:551) (the &#147;Swedish Companies Act&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Other than being of legal age, there are no age limit restrictions for directors and they are not required to own any shares in the Company.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Share Capital, Increases of Share Capital and Preferential Rights of Shareholders</I></B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Articles of Association of Ericsson provide that the share capital of the Company may not be less than SEK 6,000,000,000 nor more than SEK
24,000,000,000, and that the number of shares in the Company shall amount to no less than 3,000,000,000 and no more than 12,000,000,000. As of March&nbsp;29, 2019, the registered share capital is SEK 16,670,758,678 and the Company has in total
issued 3,334,151,735 shares. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company&#146;s shares are divided into three series: Class&nbsp;A shares, Class&nbsp;B shares and
Class&nbsp;C shares; however, no Class&nbsp;C shares are currently outstanding. Under the Swedish Companies Act, shareholders must approve each issue of additional shares either by deciding on the share issue at a shareholders&#146; meeting, or by a
shareholders&#146; approval of a decision on a share issue by the Board, or by giving an authorization to the Board to decide about a share issue. If we decide to issue new Class&nbsp;A, Class&nbsp;B or Class&nbsp;C shares by means of a cash issue,
or an issue against payment through <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">set-off</FONT> of claims, Class&nbsp;A, Class&nbsp;B and Class&nbsp;C shareholders (except for Ericsson and its subsidiaries, in the event they hold shares in Ericsson) have a
primary preferential right to subscribe for new shares of the same type in relation to the number of shares previously held by them. Shares not subscribed for through a preferential right shall be offered to all shareholders for subscription on a
pro rata basis. If we decide to issue new shares of only one series by means of a cash issue or an issue against payment through <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">set-off</FONT> of claims, all shareholders, regardless of whether their shares are
Class&nbsp;A, Class&nbsp;B or Class&nbsp;C, are entitled to a preferential right to subscribe for new shares in proportion to the number of shares previously held by them. Shareholders may vote to waive shareholders&#146; preferential rights at a
general meeting of shareholders. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">25 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If we decide to issue warrants or convertibles through a cash issue or an issue against
payment through <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">set-off</FONT> of claims, the shareholders have preferential rights to subscribe to warrants as if the issue were of the shares that may be subscribed to pursuant to the warrant and, respectively,
preferential rights to subscribe to convertibles as if the issue were of the shares that the convertibles may be converted to. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The above
does not constitute any restriction to waive the shareholders&#146; preferential rights when deciding on either an issue of shares, warrants or convertibles by means of a cash issue or an issue against payment through
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">set-off</FONT> of claims. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Dividends</I></B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our Class&nbsp;A and Class&nbsp;B shareholders have the same right to dividends. Class&nbsp;C shareholders do not have any right to dividends,
as described in article 6 of our Articles of Association. No Class&nbsp;C shares are currently outstanding. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under Swedish law, only a
general meeting of shareholders may decide on payment of dividends, which may not exceed the amount proposed by the Board of Directors (except in certain limited circumstances), and may only be paid from funds legally available for that purpose.
Under Swedish law, no interim dividends may be paid in respect of any fiscal period for which audited financial statements of the company have not yet been adopted by the annual general meeting of shareholders. The market practice in Sweden is most
often for dividends to be paid annually. Under the Swedish Companies Act, dividends to shareholders and other transfers of value from a company&#151;such as purchases of its own shares (see below)&#151;may only be made in case the company&#146;s
restricted equity remains fully covered after the transfer of value has been made. The calculation shall be based upon the most recently adopted balance sheet, and any changes in the restricted equity that has occurred after the balance sheet date
shall be taken into account. In addition, dividends to shareholders and other transfers of value from the company may only be made if this is justifiable taking into account the type of business activities of the company, the scope and risks related
thereto and the company&#146;s need for financial resources, its liquidity and financial position. In respect of parent companies, also the business activities of the group, their scope and risks related thereto and the group&#146;s need for
financial resources, its liquidity and financial position shall be taken into account. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company&#146;s shares are registered in the
computerized book-entry share registration system administered by Euroclear Sweden AB (&#147;Euroclear&#148;). The rights attached to shares eligible for dividends accrue to those persons whose names are recorded in the register of shareholders on
the record day. The dividends are then sent to a specified account as directed by the person registered with Euroclear, or to the address of that person. The relevant record day must, in most circumstances, be specified in the resolution declaring a
dividend or resolving upon a capital increase or any similar matter in which shareholders have preferential rights, or the Board of Directors must be authorized to determine the relevant record day. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Where the registered holder is a nominee, the nominee receives, for the account of the beneficial owner, dividends and, on issues of shares
with preferential rights for the shareholders, shares, as well as rights. Dividends are remitted in a single payment to the nominee who is responsible for the distribution of such dividends to the beneficial owner. A similar procedure is adopted for
share issues. Specific authority to act as a nominee must be obtained from Euroclear. At the request of Euroclear, the nominee must provide information about all beneficial holders of shares to Euroclear. Euroclear is required to keep a register
with regard to any holding on behalf of a single beneficial owner in excess of 500 shares in any one company. This list is prepared every third month and must reveal the names of the beneficial owner and be open to public inspection. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Voting</I></B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In a
general meeting of shareholders of Ericsson, each Class&nbsp;A share shall carry one vote, each Class&nbsp;B share one tenth of one vote and each Class&nbsp;C share <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-thousandth</FONT> of one vote. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We are required to publish notices to attend annual general meetings no earlier than six weeks and no later than four weeks prior to the
annual general meeting and the same notice period requirements apply regarding extraordinary general meetings concerning changes in our articles of association. Notices to attend other types of extraordinary general meetings at Ericsson must be
published no earlier than six weeks and no later than three weeks prior to the general meeting. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">26 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Directors are elected during the annual general meeting for a period of one year at a time
and do not stand for reelection at staggered intervals. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A shareholder may attend and vote at the meeting in person or by proxy. For
companies whose shares are registered in a central securities depositary register, proxies are valid for up to five years from the date of issuance. Any shareholder wishing to attend a general meeting must notify us no later than on the day
specified in the notice. We are required to accept all notifications of attendance received at least five business days (Saturdays normally included) prior to the meeting. A person designated in the register as a nominee (including the depositary of
the ADSs) is not entitled to vote at a general meeting, nor is a beneficial owner whose share is registered in the name of a nominee (including the depositary of the ADSs) unless the beneficial owner first arranges to have such owner&#146;s own name
entered in the register of shareholders maintained by Euroclear no later than the designated record day. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the Swedish Companies Act,
elections are determined by a plurality vote. Resolutions, other than elections, are passed by a simple majority of votes cast at the meeting with the chairman of the meeting having a decisive vote, unless otherwise required by law or a
company&#146;s articles of association. Under the Swedish Companies Act, certain resolutions require special quorums and majorities, including, but not limited to, the following: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B></B><B>a)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">a resolution to amend the articles of association requires a majority of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-thirds</FONT> of the votes cast as well as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-thirds</FONT> of the shares represented at the meeting, except in those circumstances described in b&#151;d below;
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B></B><B>b)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">a resolution to amend the articles of association which reduces any shareholder&#146;s rights to profits or
assets, restricts the transferability of shares or alters the legal relationship between shares, normally requires the unanimous approval of the shareholders present at the meeting and who hold nine-tenths of all outstanding shares;
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>c)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">a resolution to amend the articles of association for the purpose of limiting the number of shares with which a
shareholder may vote at a general meeting or allocating part of the net profit for the fiscal year to a restricted fund or limiting the use of the company&#146;s profits or assets in a liquidation or dissolution, normally requires the approval of
shareholders representing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-thirds</FONT> of the votes cast and nine-tenths of the shares represented at the meeting; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>d)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">a resolution of the kind referred to under B or C above may, however, be taken with a lower supermajority
requirement if the amendments referred to therein will only adversely affect specific shares or classes of shares. In such cases, the requirement under a above will apply together with the following separate supermajority: (a)&nbsp;where only a
class of shares is adversely affected, approval of the owners of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-half</FONT> of all shares of such class and nine-tenths of the shares of such class represented at the meeting, or (b)&nbsp;where the shares
adversely affected do not constitute a class of shares, the unanimous approval of all such affected outstanding shares present at the meeting and who hold nine-tenths of all outstanding shares adversely affected; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>e)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">a resolution to issue, approve or authorize the issuance for cash of new shares, warrants or convertibles with
a deviation from the preferential right for existing shareholders requires a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-thirds</FONT> majority of votes cast at the meeting as well as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-thirds</FONT> of the shares
represented at the meeting; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
